<p>The <b>2016 AFC U-23 Championship qualification</b> was a men's under-23 <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> competition which decided the participating teams of the <a href="/wiki/2016_AFC_U-23_Championship" title="2016 AFC U-23 Championship">2016 AFC U-23 Championship</a>. Players born on or after 1 January 1993 were eligible to compete in the tournament.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-regulations_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-1">[1]</a></sup></p>
<p>A total of 16 teams qualified to play in the final tournament, including <a href="/wiki/Qatar_national_under-23_football_team" title="Qatar national under-23 football team">Qatar</a> who qualified automatically as hosts.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-host_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-host-2">[2]</a></sup></p>
<p>The top three teams of the final tournament qualified for the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2016_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2016 Summer Olympics – Men's tournament">2016 Summer Olympics men's football tournament</a> in Brazil.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rio2016_3-0"><a href="#cite_note-Rio2016-3">[3]</a></sup></p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Draw">Draw</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_AFC_U-23_Championship_qualification&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Draw">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The draw for the qualifiers was held on 4 December 2014, 11:00 <a href="/wiki/UTC%2B08:00" title="UTC+08:00">UTC+8</a>, at the AFC House in <a href="/wiki/Kuala_Lumpur" title="Kuala Lumpur">Kuala Lumpur</a>, <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup> A total of 43 <a href="/wiki/Asian_Football_Confederation" title="Asian Football Confederation">AFC</a> member national teams entered the qualifying stage and were drawn into ten groups.</p>
<ul>
<li>West Zone had 23 entrants from <a href="/wiki/Central_Asian_Football_Association" title="Central Asian Football Association">Central Asia</a>, <a href="/wiki/South_Asian_Football_Federation" title="South Asian Football Federation">South Asia</a> and <a href="/wiki/West_Asian_Football_Federation" title="West Asian Football Federation">West Asia</a> (excluding hosts Qatar who did not enter the qualifying stage), where they were drawn into three groups of five teams and two groups of four teams</li>
<li>East Zone had 20 entrants from <a href="/wiki/ASEAN_Football_Federation" title="ASEAN Football Federation">ASEAN</a> and <a href="/wiki/East_Asian_Football_Federation" title="East Asian Football Federation">East Asia</a>, where they were drawn into five groups of four teams.</li>
</ul>
<p>The teams were seeded according to their performance in the previous season in 2013.</p>

</tr>
<tr>
<th>West Zone<br/>
<span class="nowrap">(Groups A–E)</span></th>
<td valign="top">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_AFC_U-23_Championship_qualification&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In each group, teams played each other once at a centralised venue. The ten group winners and the best five runners-up from all groups qualified for the final tournament.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tiebreakers">Tiebreakers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_AFC_U-23_Championship_qualification&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Tiebreakers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The teams were ranked according to <a href="/wiki/Three_points_for_a_win" title="Three points for a win">points</a> (3 points for a win, 1 point for a draw, 0 points for a loss). If tied on points, tiebreakers would be applied in the following order:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-regulations_1-1"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-1">[1]</a></sup></p>
<ol>
<li>Greater number of points obtained in the group matches between the teams concerned;</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Goal_difference" title="Goal difference">Goal difference</a> resulting from the group matches between the teams concerned;</li>
<li>Greater number of goals scored in the group matches between the teams concerned;</li>
<li>If, after applying criteria 1 to 3, teams still have an equal ranking, criteria 1 to 3 are reapplied exclusively to the matches between the teams in question to determine their final rankings. If this procedure does not lead to a decision, criteria 5 to 9 apply;</li>
<li>Goal difference in all the group matches;</li>
<li>Greater number of goals scored in all the group matches;</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">Penalty shoot-out</a> if only two teams are involved and they are both on the field of play;</li>
<li>Fewer score calculated according to the number of yellow and red cards received in the group matches (1 point for a single yellow card, 3 points for a red card as a consequence of two yellow cards, 3 points for a direct red card, 4 points for a yellow card followed by a direct red card);</li>
<li>Drawing of lots.</li>
</ol>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Group_stage">Group stage</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_AFC_U-23_Championship_qualification&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Group stage">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The matches were played between 23–31 March 2015 for Groups A and C (five-team groups); 27–31 March 2015 for Groups D–J (four-team groups); 16–20 May 2015 for Group B (due to postponement).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup></p>
<table class="wikitable">
<tr>
<th>Legend</th>
</tr>
<tr style="background-color:#BBF3BB;">
<td>Group winners and <a href="#Ranking_of_second-placed_teams">best five runners-up</a> qualify for the <a href="/wiki/2016_AFC_U-23_Championship" title="2016 AFC U-23 Championship">finals</a></td>
</tr>
</table>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Group_A">Group A</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_AFC_U-23_Championship_qualification&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Group A">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>All matches were held in <a href="/wiki/Oman" title="Oman">Oman</a>.</li>
<li>Times listed were <a href="/wiki/UTC%2B04:00" title="UTC+04:00">UTC+4</a>.</li>
</ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Group_B">Group B</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_AFC_U-23_Championship_qualification&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Group B">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>All matches were originally scheduled to be held in <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>, between 23–31 March 2015 at <a href="/wiki/Punjab_Stadium" title="Punjab Stadium">Punjab Stadium</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lahore" title="Lahore">Lahore</a>, but were postponed due to safety and security reasons after <a href="/wiki/Lahore_church_bombings" title="Lahore church bombings">bombings and civil unrest in the city</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li>All matches were later scheduled to be held in the <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates" title="United Arab Emirates">United Arab Emirates</a> between 16–24 May 2015.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup> After the withdrawal of Turkmenistan, the dates were shortened to 16–20 May 2015.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup></li>
<li>Times listed were <a href="/wiki/UTC%2B04:00" title="UTC+04:00">UTC+4</a>.</li>
</ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ranking_of_second-placed_teams">Ranking of second-placed teams</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2016_AFC_U-23_Championship_qualification&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Ranking of second-placed teams">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In order to ensure equality when comparing the runner-up team of all groups, the results of the matches against the 5th-placed team in Groups A and C were ignored due to the other groups having only four teams.</p>
<p>The best runner-up teams among those ranked second in the groups were determined as follows:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-regulations_1-2"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-1">[1]</a></sup></p>
<ol>
<li>Greater number of points obtained from group matches identified by AFC;</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Goal_difference" title="Goal difference">Goal difference</a> resulting from group matches identified by AFC;</li>
<li>Greater number of goals scored in group matches identified by AFC;</li>
<li>Greater number of wins in group matches identified by AFC;</li>
<li>Fewer score calculated according to the number of yellow and red cards received in group matches identified by AFC (1 point for a single yellow card, 3 points for a red card as a consequence of two yellow cards, 3 points for a direct red card, 4 points for a yellow card followed by a direct red card);</li>
<li>Drawing of lots.</li>
</ol>
